&nbsp; procedure actChangeMagnetizeExecute(Sender: TObject);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; procedure updateCanvasSizeWithCoords(x,y: Integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; public</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; PBW, PBH: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; FScale: Real;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; procedure useScale(var x,y: integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; procedure DiscardScale(var x,y: integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; procedure SD_Resize;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; function getFigureHead:PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; function openFile(mode: TFileMode):string;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; function saveFile(mode: TFileMode):string;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; procedure changeCanvasSize(w,h: Integer; flag: Boolean = true);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; procedure getCanvasSIze(var w,h:Integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; EditorForm: TEditorForm;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; FigHead: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; CurrType: TType;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; CurrLineType: TLineType;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; CurrFigure, ClickFigure: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tempX, tempY: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; DM: TDrawMode;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; EM: TEditMode;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; prevText:String;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; currPointAdr: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; CoppyFigure: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; //FT: TFigureType;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">implementation</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">{$R *.dfm}</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">{$R HTML.RES}</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">{$R+}</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">{$R-}</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">uses FCanvasSizeSettings, FHtmlView, Model.Files;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure TEditorForm.changeEditorText(newtext: string);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; edtRectText.text := newtext</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure TEditorForm.switchChangedStatus(flag: Boolean);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; isChanged := flag;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Select the scale of the image</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure TEditorForm.tbSelectScaleChange(Sender: TObject);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; case (Sender as TTrackBar).Position of</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 1: FScale := 0.1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 2: FScale := 0.3;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 3: FScale := 0.5;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 4: FScale := 0.8;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 5: FScale := 1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 6: FScale := 1.2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 7: FScale := 1.5;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 8: FScale := 1.7;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 9: FScale := 2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; 10: FScale := 4;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; lblScaleView.Caption := &#39; &nbsp;&#39; + IntToStr( Round(FScale*100) ) + &#39;%&#39;;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; changeCanvasSize(PBW, PBH);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Self.Invalidate;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure TEditorForm.updateCanvasSizeWithCoords(x, y: Integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; pbMain.Width := x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; pbMain.Height := y; </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; pbMain.Repaint;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure TEditorForm.useScale(var x, y: integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; x := Round(FScale*x);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; y := Round(FScale*y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure TEditorForm.pbMainMouseDown(Sender: TObject; Button: TMouseButton;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Shift: TShiftState; X, Y: Integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var x0, y0: Integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; UndoRec: TUndoStackInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin &nbsp;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; x0 := x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; y0 := y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; roundCoords(x,y); // round coords (Use steps)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if dm = DrawLine then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; case button of</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; TMouseButton.mbLeft:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // Add new point of current line:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.PrevPointAdr := addNewPoint( CurrFigure^.Info.PointHead, Round(x / FScale),Round(y / FScale));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // CHANGES STASCK PUSHING START</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.ChangeType := chAddPoint;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.adr := CurrFigure;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoStackPush(USVertex, UndoRec);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isChanged := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; actUndo.Enabled := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // CHANGES STASCK PUSHING END</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // If clicked button - right or middle then finish drawing</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; TMouseButton.mbRight: </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // Remove lines with one point</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; endDrawLine;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; TMouseButton.mbMiddle: endDrawLine;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; DM := Draw; // Begin Drawing</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; // If </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if (EM = NoEdit) and (CurrType &lt;&gt; None) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; isChanged := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; // if at the moment nothing draws, start drawing</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if CurrType &lt;&gt; Line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // Add new figure to canvas</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; CurrFigure := addFigure(FigHead, Round(x/FScale),Round(y/FSCale), CurrType, edtRectText.Text);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // CHANGES STACK PUSHING START</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.ChangeType := chInsert;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.adr := Currfigure;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; CurrFigure.Info.y1 := y - abs(CurrFigure.Info.y1 - CurrFigure.Info.y2) div 2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoStackPush(USVertex, UndoRec);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; actUndo.Enabled := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // CHANGES STACK PUSHING END</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; else if (DM &lt;&gt; DrawLine) and (Button = mbLeft) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // Add new lines to canvas</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; CurrFigure := addLine(FigHead, Round(x/FScale),Round(y/FScale));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // CHANGES STASCK PUSHING START</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.ChangeType := chInsert;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.adr := Currfigure;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; DM := DrawLine;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoStackPush(USVertex, UndoRec);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; actUndo.Enabled := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // CHANGES STASCK PUSHING END</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tempx:= x; // Update coordinates for moving</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tempy:= y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; // If the click occurred on the figure, we put the current variable in the </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; // appropriate variable</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ClickFigure := getClickFigure(Round(x0/FScale) ,Round(y0/FScale), FigHead);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if (ClickFigure &lt;&gt; nil) and (ClickFigure^.Info.tp &lt;&gt; line) and (CurrFigure &lt;&gt; nil)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and (CurrFigure^.Info.tp &lt;&gt; line) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; // We paste into the text field with the text of the figure the text of the current shape</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; changeEditorText(String(ClickFigure^.Info.Txt));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; changeEditorText(prevText);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure changeCursor(ScrollBox:TScrollBox; Mode: TEditMode);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; case mode of</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; NoEdit: ScrollBox.Cursor := crArrow;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Move: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeAll;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; TSide: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeNS;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; BSide: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeNS;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; RSide: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeWE;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; LSide: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeWE;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Vert1: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeNWSE;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Vert2: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeNESW;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Vert3: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeNESW;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Vert4: ScrollBox.Cursor := crSizeNWSE;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp:integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if (R&lt;&gt;nil) and (R^.Info.tp &lt;&gt; Line) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if y1 &gt; y2 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &#1082;&#1086;&#1087;&#1080;&#1080; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1099;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure copyFigure(head: PFigList; copyfigure:PFigList);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &#1074; &#1079;&#1072;&#1074;&#1080;&#1089;&#1080;&#1084;&#1086;&#1089;&#1090;&#1080; &#1086;&#1090; &#1090;&#1086;&#1075;&#1086;,</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1063;&#1090;&#1086; &#1085;&#1072;&#1093;&#1086;&#1076;&#1080;&#1090;&#1089;&#1103; &#1074;&#1086; &#1082;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090;&#1072;&#1084; &#1085;&#1072;&#1074;&#1077;&#1076;&#1077;&#1085;&#1080;&#1103; &#1084;&#1099;&#1096;&#1080;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function getEditMode(status: TDrawMode; x,y: Integer; head: PFigList; CT: TType) :TEditMode;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; r:TFigureInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpPoint: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp := head;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while temp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; R := temp^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if (status = nodraw) and (R.tp &lt;&gt; Line) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ( (x &gt; R.x1) and (x &lt; R.x2) and (y &gt; R.y1) and (y &lt; R.y2)) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1042;&#1085;&#1091;&#1090;&#1088;&#1080; &#1086;&#1073;&#1098;&#1077;&#1082;&#1090;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := Move;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1047;&#1072; &#1087;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1077;&#1083;&#1072;&#1084;&#1080; &#1086;&#1073;&#1098;&#1077;&#1082;&#1090;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := NoEdit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ( (x &gt; R.x1) and (x &lt; R.x2) and ((abs(y - R.y1) &lt; Tolerance) or (abs(y - R.y2) &lt; Tolerance))) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1043;&#1086;&#1088;&#1080;&#1079;&#1086;&#1085;&#1090;&#1072;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1072;&#1103; &#1089;&#1090;&#1086;&#1088;&#1086;&#1085;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(y - R.y1) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := TSide</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result:= BSide;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ( (y &gt; R.y1) and (y &lt; R.y2) and ((abs(x - R.x1) &lt; Tolerance) or (abs(x - R.x2) &lt; Tolerance))) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1042;&#1077;&#1088;&#1090;&#1080;&#1082;&#1072;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1072;&#1103; &#1089;&#1090;&#1086;&#1088;&#1086;&#1085;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(x - R.x1) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := Lside</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result:= RSide;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if ((abs(y-R.y1) &lt; Tolerance) and (abs(x-R.x1) &lt; Tolerance)) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1051;&#1077;&#1074;&#1072;&#1103; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1093;&#1085;&#1103;&#1103; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1096;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := Vert1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(y-R.y1) &lt; Tolerance) and (abs(x-R.x2) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1055;&#1088;&#1072;&#1074;&#1072;&#1103; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1093;&#1085;&#1103;&#1103; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1096;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := Vert2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(y-R.y2) &lt; Tolerance) and (abs(x-R.x1) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1051;&#1077;&#1074;&#1072;&#1103; &#1085;&#1080;&#1078;&#1085;&#1103;&#1103; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1096;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := Vert3;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(y-R.y2) &lt; Tolerance) and (abs(x-R.x2) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1055;&#1088;&#1072;&#1074;&#1072;&#1103; &#1085;&#1080;&#1078;&#1085;&#1103;&#1103; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1096;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := Vert4;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // ?? ?? ??? ?? ??? ?? ?? \\</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if result &lt;&gt; NoEdit then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; CurrFigure := temp;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; else if (status = nodraw) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpPoint := R.PointHead;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; while tmpPoint &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(y-tmpPoint^.Info.y) &lt; Tolerance) and (abs(x-tmpPoint^.Info.x) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; CurrFigure := temp;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; currPointAdr := tmpPoint;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := Move;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; { ToDo: KEK }</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpPoint := tmpPoint^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (CT = &nbsp;TType(4)) and (isBelongsLine(temp^.Info.PointHead, x,y)) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; CurrFigure := temp;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := LineMove;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; temp := temp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Result := &nbsp;NoEdit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1054;&#1082;&#1088;&#1091;&#1075;&#1083;&#1077;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077; &#1082;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090; &#1089; &#1079;&#1072;&#1076;&#1072;&#1085;&#1085;&#1099;&#1084; &#1096;&#1072;&#1075;&#1086;&#1084;.</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure roundCoords(var x,y:integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; temp:=temp2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; head.Adr := nil;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1056;&#1077;&#1076;&#1072;&#1082;&#1090;&#1080;&#1088;&#1086;&#1074;&#1072;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077; begin</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Move: // &#1055;&#1077;&#1088;&#1077;&#1084;&#1077;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1084; &#1086;&#1073;&#1098;&#1077;&#1082;&#1090; :)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if F^.Info.tp = Line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oldp:= currPointAdr^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; currPointAdr^.Info.x := currPointAdr^.Info.x - (TmpX - x);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; currPointAdr^.Info.y := currPointAdr^.Info.y - (Tmpy - y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; MoveLine(CurrFigure^.Info.PointHead, oldp, currPointAdr^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1057;&#1084;&#1077;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1084; &#1086;&#1073;&#1098;&#1077;&#1082;&#1090;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // TmpX, TmpY - &#1089;&#1084;&#1077;&#1097;&#1077;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077; &#1082;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090; &#1086;&#1090;&#1085;&#1086;&#1089;&#1080;&#1090;&#1077;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1086; &#1087;&#1088;&#1086;&#1096;&#1083;&#1086;&#1075;&#1086; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.y2 := F^.Info.y2 - (TmpY - y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; LineMove:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; moveALlLinePoint(CurrFigure^.Info.PointHead, (TmpX - x), (Tmpy - y));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1093;&#1085;&#1102;&#1102; &#1089;&#1090;&#1086;&#1088;&#1086;&#1085;&#1091;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.y1 := F^.Info.y1 - (Tmpy - y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &#1087;&#1088;&#1072;&#1074;&#1091;&#1102; &#1089;&#1090;&#1086;&#1088;&#1086;&#1085;&#1091;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.x2 := F^.Info.x2 - (Tmpx - x);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.y1 := F^.Info.y1 - (Tmpy - y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Vert2:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.x2 := F^.Info.x2 - (TmpX - x);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.y1 := F^.Info.y1 - (Tmpy - y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Vert3:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.x1 := F^.Info.x1 - (TmpX - x);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.y2 := F^.Info.y2 - (Tmpy - y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Vert4:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.x2 := F^.Info.x2 - (TmpX - x);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; F^.Info.y2 := F^.Info.y2 - (Tmpy - y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1060;&#1091;&#1085;&#1082;&#1094;&#1080;&#1103; &quot;&#1055;&#1088;&#1080;&#1084;&#1072;&#1075;&#1085;&#1080;&#1095;&#1080;&#1074;&#1072;&#1077;&#1090;&quot; &#1090;&#1086;&#1095;&#1082;&#1091; &#1082; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1077; &#1080; &#1074;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1090; true, &#1077;&#1089;&#1083;&#1080;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &quot;&#1087;&#1088;&#1080;&#1084;&#1072;&#1075;&#1085;&#1080;&#1095;&#1080;&#1074;&#1072;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077;&quot; &#1091;&#1076;&#1072;&#1083;&#1086;&#1089;&#1100;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function magnetizeWithFigures(head: PFigList; Point: PPointsList):boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp := head^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Result := false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while temp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if temp^.Info.tp &lt;&gt; Line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs( Point^.Info.x - temp^.Info.x1) &lt; NearFigure) // &#1051;&#1077;&#1074;&#1072;&#1103; &#1075;&#1088;&#1072;&#1085;&#1100;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ( Point^.Info.y &lt; temp^.Info.y2 )</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ( Point^.Info.y &gt; temp^.Info.y1 )</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point^.info.x := temp^.Info.x1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point^.Info.y := (temp^.Info.y1 + temp^.Info.y2) div 2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end else if (abs( Point^.Info.x - temp^.Info.x2) &lt; NearFigure) &nbsp;// &#1055;&#1088;&#1072;&#1074;&#1072;&#1103; &#1075;&#1088;&#1072;&#1085;&#1100;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ( Point^.Info.y &lt; temp^.Info.y2 )</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ( Point^.Info.y &gt; temp^.Info.y1 )</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point^.info.x := temp^.Info.x2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point^.Info.y := (temp^.Info.y1 + temp^.Info.y2) div 2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; temp := temp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1055;&#1086;&#1080;&#1089;&#1082; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;, &#1088;&#1072;&#1089;&#1087;&#1086;&#1083;&#1086;&#1078;&#1077;&#1085;&#1085;&#1099;&#1093; &#1087;&#1088;&#1080;&#1073;&#1083;&#1080;&#1079;&#1080;&#1090;&#1077;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1086; &#1074; &#1086;&#1076;&#1085;&#1091; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1102;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1048; &#1080;&#1079;&#1084;&#1077;&#1085;&#1077;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077; &#1082;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090; &#1090;&#1072;&#1082;, &#1095;&#1090;&#1086;&#1073;&#1099; &#1086;&#1085;&#1080; &#1086;&#1082;&#1072;&#1079;&#1072;&#1083;&#1080;&#1089;&#1100; &#1090;&#1086;&#1095;&#1085;&#1086;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1074; &#1086;&#1076;&#1085;&#1086;&#1081; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1080;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure SearchFiguresInOneLine(head, curr: PFigList);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var &nbsp; </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; CurrY : Integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tempY : integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; with curr^.Info do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; CurrY := y1 + (y2 - y1) div 2; // &#1062;&#1077;&#1085;&#1090;&#1088; &#1087;&#1086; Y &#1087;&#1077;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1072;&#1085;&#1085;&#1086;&#1081; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1099;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp := head^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while temp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if (temp^.Info.tp = line) or (temp = curr) then </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; temp := temp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; with temp^.Info do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tempY := y1 + (y2 - y1) div 2; // &#1062;&#1077;&#1085;&#1090;&#1088; &#1087;&#1086; Y &#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1091;&#1097;&#1077;&#1081; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1099;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if abs( CurrY - tempY ) &lt; NearFigure then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; temp^.Info.y1 := curry - (Temp^.Info.y2 - Temp^.Info.y1) div 2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; temp^.Info.y2 := curry + (Temp^.Info.y2 - Temp^.Info.y1) div 2; </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; temp := temp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; </span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &quot;&#1055;&#1088;&#1080;&#1084;&#1072;&#1075;&#1085;&#1080;&#1095;&#1080;&#1074;&#1072;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077;&quot; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1081; &#1082; &#1076;&#1088;&#1091;&#1075;&#1080;&#1084; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1072;&#1084;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure MagnetizeLines(head: PFigList);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpP: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; NearP: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; x,y : integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; oldP, newP: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; prevP: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp := head^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while tmp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if tmp^.Info.tp &lt;&gt; Line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; SearchFiguresInOneLine(head, tmp); // &#1055;&#1088;&#1086;&#1073;&#1091;&#1077;&#1084; &#1085;&#1072;&#1081;&#1090;&#1080; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1099; &#1074; &#1086;&#1076;&#1085;&#1091; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1102;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; prevP:=nil;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP:= tmP^.Info.PointHead^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; while tmpP &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; x := tmpP^.Info.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; y := tmpP^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1055;&#1088;&#1086;&#1073;&#1091;&#1077;&#1084; &#1087;&#1088;&#1080;&#1084;&#1072;&#1075;&#1085;&#1080;&#1090;&#1080;&#1090;&#1100; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1102; &#1082; &#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1089;&#1090;&#1086;&#1074;&#1086;&#1081; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1077;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (isHorLine(tmpP, prevP)) and (magnetizeWithFigures(head, tmpP)) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oldp.x := x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oldp.y := y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; MoveLine(tmp^.Info.PointHead,oldP, tmpP^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP := tmpP^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1055;&#1088;&#1086;&#1073;&#1091;&#1077;&#1084; &#1087;&#1088;&#1080;&#1084;&#1075;&#1085;&#1080;&#1090;&#1080;&#1090;&#1100; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1102; &#1082; &#1076;&#1088;&#1091;&#1075;&#1086;&#1081; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1080;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; NearP := searchNearLine(head, x,y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if NearP &lt;&gt; nil then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oldp.x := tmpP^.Info.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; oldp.y := tmpP^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; newP.x := nearP.Info.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; newP.y := tmpP^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if abs(tmpP^.Info.x &nbsp;- nearP.Info.x) &lt; nearFigure then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP^.Info := newP;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; MoveLine(tmp^.Info.PointHead,oldP, tmpP^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; newP.x := tmpP^.Info.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; newP.y := nearP.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if abs(tmpP^.Info.y - nearP.Info.y) &lt; nearFigure then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP^.Info := newP;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; MoveLine(tmp^.Info.PointHead,oldP, tmpP^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prevP := tmpP;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP := tmpP^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1054;&#1090;&#1084;&#1077;&#1085;&#1072; &#1080;&#1079;&#1084;&#1077;&#1085;&#1077;&#1085;&#1080;&#1081;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure undoChanges(UndoRec: TUndoStackInfo; Canvas: TCanvas);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpP: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; case UndoRec.ChangeType of</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; chDelete:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1057;&#1085;&#1086;&#1074;&#1072; &#1074;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1084; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1091; (&#1054;&#1085;&#1072; &#1085;&#1077; &#1073;&#1099;&#1083;&#1072; &#1091;&#1076;&#1072;&#1083;&#1077;&#1085;&#1072; &#1092;&#1080;&#1079;&#1080;&#1095;&#1077;&#1089;&#1082;&#1080;, &#1090;&#1086;&#1083;&#1100;&#1082;&#1086; &#1083;&#1086;&#1075;&#1080;&#1095;&#1077;&#1089;&#1082;&#1080;)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := UndoRec.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp.Adr := UndoRec.PrevFigure^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; undoRec.PrevFigure^.Adr := tmp;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; chAddPoint:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1059;&#1076;&#1072;&#1083;&#1077;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077; &#1090;&#1086;&#1095;&#1082;&#1080; (&#1092;&#1080;&#1079;&#1080;&#1095;&#1077;&#1089;&#1082;&#1086;&#1077;)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP:= UndoRec.PrevPointAdr^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.PrevPointAdr^.Adr := nil;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Dispose(tmpP);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; chInsert:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1059;&#1076;&#1072;&#1083;&#1077;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1099;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; removeFigure(EditorForm.getFigureHead, UndoRec.adr)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; chFigMove:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1042;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1090; &#1087;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1099;&#1076;&#1091;&#1097;&#1080;&#1093; &#1082;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1099;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.adr^.Info := UndoRec.PrevInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; chPointMove:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1042;&#1086;&#1074;&#1079;&#1088;&#1072;&#1090; &#1087;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1099;&#1076;&#1091;&#1097;&#1080;&#1093; &#1082;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090; &#1090;&#1086;&#1095;&#1077;&#1082; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1080;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; changeLineCoordsFromStr(UndoRec.adr^.Info.PointHead, UndoRec.st);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; chChangeText:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1042;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1090; &#1087;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1099;&#1076;&#1091;&#1097;&#1077;&#1075;&#1086; &#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1089;&#1090;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; UndoRec.adr^.Info.Txt := UndoRec.text;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; chCanvasSize:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1042;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1090; &#1087;&#1088;&#1086;&#1096;&#1083;&#1099;&#1093; &#1088;&#1072;&#1079;&#1084;&#1077;&#1088;&#1086;&#1074; &#1087;&#1086;&#1083;&#1086;&#1090;&#1085;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; EditorForm.changeCanvasSize(UndoRec.w, UndoRec.h, false);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; - &#1077;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1089;&#1090;&#1074;&#1077;&#1085;&#1085;&#1072;&#1103; &#1080; &#1092;&#1080;&#1075;&#1091;&#1088;&#1072; &#1076;&#1086;&#1088;&#1080;&#1089;&#1086;&#1074;&#1072;&#1085;&#1072; &#1090;&#1086;&#1095;&#1082;&#1080; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1080;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function addNewPoint(var head: PPointsList; x,y:integer):PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; py := tmp^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1047;&#1072;&#1087;&#1088;&#1077;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1084; &#1087;&#1088;&#1086;&#1074;&#1086;&#1076;&#1080;&#1090;&#1100; &#1087;&#1088;&#1103;&#1084;&#1091;&#1102; &#1087;&#1086;&#1076; &#1091;&#1075;&#1083;&#1086;&#1084;.</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; try</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; (&#1042;&#1089;&#1077; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1080; &#1074; &#1089;&#1080;&#1085;&#1090;&#1072;&#1082;&#1089;&#1080;&#1095;&#1077;&#1089;&#1082;&#1080;&#1093; &#1076;&#1080;&#1072;&#1075;&#1088;&#1072;&#1084;&#1084;&#1072;&#1093;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1044;&#1086;&#1083;&#1078;&#1085;&#1099; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1085;&#1077;&#1090; nil</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function searchNearLine(head: PFigList; var x,y: integer):PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;(y &gt; minY)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;(y &lt; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := tmpP;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;(y &gt; minY)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;(y &lt; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(MinY - Y) &lt; NearFigure)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;(X &gt; minX)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;(X &lt; maxX) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Y := MinY;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := tmpP;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; temp := temp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// BOOOLEAN FUNCTIONS</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1042;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1090; true &#1077;&#1089;&#1083;&#1080; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1103; &#1075;&#1086;&#1088;&#1080;&#1079;&#1086;&#1085;&#1090;&#1072;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1072;&#1103;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function isHorLine(curr, prev: PPointsList):boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if prev = nil then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Result := (curr^.Adr &lt;&gt; nil) and (curr^.Info.y = curr^.adr^.Info.y)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Result := prev^.Info.y = curr^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1042;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1090; true &#1077;&#1089;&#1083;&#1080; &#1085;&#1091;&#1078;&#1085;&#1072; &#1089;&#1090;&#1088;&#1077;&#1083;&#1082;&#1072; &#1087;&#1086; &#1089;&#1077;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1077;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function needMiddleArrow(tmp: PPointsList; FirstP: TPointsInfo) :Boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Result := (tmp^.Adr &lt;&gt; nil) and (tmp^.adr^.Adr = nil) and (tmp^.Info.x &lt;&gt; FirstP.x)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and (tmp^.Info.x = tmp^.adr^.Info.x) and (abs(tmp^.Info.y - tmp^.adr^.Info.y) &gt; Tolerance*2)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1042;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1090; true &#1077;&#1089;&#1083;&#1080; &#1085;&#1091;&#1078;&#1077;&#1085; &#1076;&#1080;&#1072;&#1075;&#1086;&#1085;&#1072;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1099;&#1081; &#1089;&#1088;&#1077;&#1079;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function isHorisontalIntersection(head: PFigList; blocked: PPointsList):boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpP: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ti1, ti2: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Result := false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp:= head^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while tmp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if tmp^.Info.tp = Line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if tmp^.info.PointHead = nil then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP := tmp^.Info.PointHead^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; while (tmpP &lt;&gt; nil) and (tmpP^.adr &lt;&gt; nil) do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ti1 := tmpP^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ti2 := tmpP^.adr.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(ti1.x- blocked.Info.x) &lt; NearFigure)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and (abs(ti2.x - blocked.Info.x) &lt; NearFigure)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and (blocked.Info.y &lt; max(ti1.y, ti2.y))</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and (blocked.Info.y &gt; min(ti1.y, ti2.y))</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; and (tmpP &lt;&gt; blocked) and (tmpP^.adr &lt;&gt; blocked)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP:= tmpP^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function isBelongsLine(head: PPointsList; x,y: integer): Boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp, tmp2 : PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if (head = nil) or (head^.Adr = nil) or (head^.Adr^.Adr = nil) then exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp := head^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp2 := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Result := false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while (tmp &lt;&gt; nil) and (tmp2 &lt;&gt; nil) do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if (tmp^.Info.x = tmp2^.Info.x) and (abs(tmp^.Info.x - x) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (y &gt; min(tmp^.Info.y, tmp2^.Info.y)) and (y &lt; max(tmp^.Info.y, tmp2^.Info.y)) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; exit</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;if (tmp^.Info.y = tmp2^.Info.y) and &nbsp;(abs(tmp^.Info.y - y) &lt; Tolerance) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (x &gt; min(tmp^.Info.x, tmp2^.Info.x)) and (x &lt; max(tmp^.Info.x, tmp2^.Info.x)) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Result := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; exit</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmp2 := tmp2^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c63">end.</span></p><p class="c25 c12"><span class="c45"></span></p><p class="c25"><span class="c45">&#1052;&#1086;&#1076;&#1091;&#1083;&#1100; &nbsp; ShowMessage(&#39;Error&#39;); // NonDelete - &#1090;&#1086;&#1083;&#1100;&#1082;&#1086; &#1089;&#1072;&#1084;&#1099;&#1081; &#1087;&#1086;&#1089;&#1083;&#1077;&#1076;&#1085;&#1080;&#1081; &#1101;&#1083;&#1077;&#1084;&#1077;&#1085;&#1090; &#1089;&#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; true &#1077;&#1089;&#1083;&#1080; &#1089;&#1090;&#1077;&#1082; &#1087;&#1091;&#1089;&#1090;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function isStackEmpty(Vertex: PUndoStack): Boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &#1089;&#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure UndoStackClear(var vertex: PUndoStack);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; x,y: integer);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var scale : real;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; scale := EditorForm.FScale;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,x-Arrow_Height,y+Arrow_Width*coef);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,x,y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,x+Arrow_Height,y+Arrow_Width*coef);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,x,y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Draw horisontal arrow</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawArrow(Canvas:TCanvas; x,y : integer; coef: ShortInt);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,x,y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp;
