ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,x,y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure selectFigure(canvas: TCanvas; head:PFigList);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp : PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; //ShowMessage(&#39;kek&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if head^.Info.tp &lt;&gt; line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1056;&#1080;&#1089;&#1091;&#1077;&#1084; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1096;&#1080;&#1085;&#1099;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; drawSelectFigure(canvas, head^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; //showmessage(&#39;kek&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if head^.Info.PointHead = nil then exit;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := head^.Info.PointHead^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; while tmp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawSelectLineVertex(canvas,tmp^.info);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Draw out bound line ( |\----- )</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawOutBoundLine(canvas: TCanvas; FirstP: TPointsInfo; tmp:PPointsList);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; coef: -1..1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if FirstP.y - tmp^.adr^.Info.y &lt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; coef := 1</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; coef := -1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x- Lines_DegLenght, tmp^.Info.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x, tmp^.Info.y+coef*Lines_Deg);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x, tmp^.Info.y+coef*Lines_Deg);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; // canvas.Rectangle(tmp^.Info.x-VertRad,tmp^.Info.y+15*coef-VertRad, tmp^.Info.x+VertRad, tmp^.Info.y+15*coef+VertRad);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Return true if this is begin of vertical line</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function beginOfVertLine(tmp:PPointsList;firstP: TPointsInfo):boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; result := (tmp^.Adr &lt;&gt; nil) and</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (FirstP.x = tmp^.adr^.Info.x) &nbsp;and // If vertical line</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; (FirstP.y &lt;&gt; tmp^.adr^.Info.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Draw rectangles at vertex of figures</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawVertexRect(canvas:TCanvas; point: TPointsInfo; color:TColor = clBlack);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleVertRad: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Pen.Color := color;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if color &lt;&gt; clBlack then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; Canvas.Brush.Color := color;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Pen.Width := 1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; EditorForm.useScale(Point.x, point.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleVertRad := ScaleRound(EditorForm.FScale, VertRad);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Rectangle(point.x-ScaleVertRad,point.y-ScaleVertRad, point.x+ScaleVertRad, point.y+ScaleVertRad);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Pen.Width := Round(Lines_Width*EditorForm.FScale);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Pen.Color := clBlack;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Brush.Color := clwhite;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Draw Incoming line ( -----/| )</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawIncomingLine(canvas: tcanvas; point: TPointsInfo; coef: ShortInt);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,point.x, point.y + (Lines_Deg*coef));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,point.x, point.y + (Lines_Deg*coef));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,point.x+Lines_DegLenght, point.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawArrowVertical(canvas, point.x, point.y+Lines_DegLenght*coef, coef);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Draw arrow at end of line</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawArrowAtEnd(canvas:TCanvas; point, PrevPoint:TPointsInfo);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpx, tmpy:integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpx := point.x - PrevPoint.x;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if tmpx &gt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; drawArrow(canvas,point.x, point.y,1)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else if tmpx &lt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; drawArrow(canvas,point.x, point.y,-1);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpy := point.y - PrevPoint.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if tmpy &gt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; drawArrowVertical(canvas,point.x, point.y,-1)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else if tmpy &lt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawArrowVertical(canvas,point.x, point.y,1);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// Draw lines</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawLines(Canvas:TCanvas; head: PPointsList; LT: TLineType; isVertex: boolean; scale: Real);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp: PPointsList; // Temp variable</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; FirstP,PrevP: TPointsInfo; // First and Prev Point in list</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpx: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; isFirstLine:boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; point1:TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; isDegEnd: boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; coef: -1..1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;//\\</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; coef := 1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Pen.Width := Trunc(Lines_Width*scale); // Width For Line</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; isFirstLine := false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp := head;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if (tmp &lt;&gt; nil) and (tmp^.Adr &lt;&gt; nil) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; FirstP.X := tmp^.Adr^.Info.x; // Initialise First Points</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; FirstP.y := tmp^.Adr^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; prevp.x := FirstP.X; // Initialise Preview Point</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; prevp.y := FirstP.Y;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x, tmp^.Info.y); // Move to first point in list</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; // FIRST POINT:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if beginOfVertLine(tmp,firstP) and (PrevP.y = tmp^.Info.y) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawOutBoundLine(canvas,FirstP, tmp);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isFirstLine := &nbsp;true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if (tmp^.Adr &lt;&gt; nil) and (PrevP.y = tmp^.adr^.Info.y) and isHorisontalIntersection(EditorForm.getFigureHead,tmp) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (tmp^.Adr &lt;&gt; nil) and (FirstP.x - tmp^.adr^.Info.x &lt; 0) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coef := 1</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coef := -1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x, tmp^.Info.y-Lines_DegLenght);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x+Lines_Deg*coef, tmp^.Info.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if isVertex then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, tmp^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; // OTHER POINTS:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; isDegEnd := false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; while tmp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; {if LT =LAdditLine then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp^.Info.y := AddY;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;}</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (PrevP.y = tmp^.Info.y) and (tmp^.Adr = nil) and &nbsp;isHorisontalIntersection(EditorForm.getFigureHead,tmp) &nbsp;then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x-Lines_Deg*coef, tmp^.Info.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1055;&#1077;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076; \ - &#1089;&#1090;&#1088;&#1077;&#1083;&#1086;&#1095;&#1082;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (PrevP.x - tmp^.Info.x &gt; 0) and (PrevP.y = tmp^.Info.y) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawArrow(canvas, tmp^.Info.x-Lines_Deg*coef, tmp^.Info.y, -1)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else if (PrevP.y = tmp^.Info.y) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawArrow(canvas, tmp^.Info.x-Lines_Deg*coef, tmp^.Info.y, 1);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x, tmp^.Info.y+Lines_DegLenght);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x-Lines_Deg*coef, tmp^.Info.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point1 := &nbsp;tmp^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isVertex then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, point1);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp:=tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isDegEnd then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawIncomingLine(canvas, tmp^.Info, coef);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isVertex then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, tmp^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp := tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleLineTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x, tmp^.Info.y);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x, tmp^.Info.y);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isVertex then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, tmp^.Info);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1056;&#1080;&#1089;&#1091;&#1077;&#1084; &#1089;&#1090;&#1088;&#1077;&#1083;&#1086;&#1095;&#1082;&#1091; &#1074; &#1082;&#1086;&#1085;&#1094;&#1077; &#1083;&#1080;&#1085;&#1080;&#1080;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (tmp^.Adr = nil) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawArrowAtEnd(canvas, tmp^.Info, prevP);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if needMiddleArrow(tmp, FirstP) then // if these is incoming and outgoing lines</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isFirstLine then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpx := tmp^.Info.x - PrevP.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if tmpx &gt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpx := 1</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpx := -1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawArrow(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x + 10 - (tmp^.Info.x - PrevP.x) div 2, tmp^.Info.y, tmpx);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ScaleMoveTo(Canvas,tmp^.Info.x , tmp^.Info.y)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if tmp^.Info.y - tmp^.adr^.Info.y &lt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coef := -1</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coef := 1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isDegEnd := true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isDegEnd:= false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prevp.x := tmp^.Info.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prevp.y := tmp^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmp:= tmp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; canvas.Pen.Width := 1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawFigure(Canvas:TCanvas; head:PFigList; scale: real; isVertex:boolean = true);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp:PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; TextW: Integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; TextH: Integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; TX, TY: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Point: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; text:string;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; temp := head^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while temp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; with temp^.Info do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if tp &lt;&gt; Line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; text := String(txt);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; case Tp of</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Def: Text := &#39;&lt; &#39; + Text + &#39; &gt; ::= &#39;;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; MetaVar: Text := &#39;&lt; &#39; + Text + &#39; &gt;&#39;;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; MetaConst: ;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; line:</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawLines(Canvas, temp^.Info.PointHead, temp^.Info.LT, isVertex, scale);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; temp := temp^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; continue; // if figure - line =&gt; draw this line and skip ineration</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; ;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Canvas.Font.Size := Font_Size;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; TextW := canvas.TextWidth(text);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; textH := Canvas.TextHeight(text);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1056;&#1072;&#1089;&#1095;&#1080;&#1090;&#1099;&#1074;&#1072;&#1077;&#1084; &#1082;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090;&#1099;, &#1095;&#1090;&#1086;&#1073;&#1099; &#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1089;&#1090; &#1073;&#1099;&#1083; &#1087;&#1086; &#1089;&#1077;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1077;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; TX := x1 + (x2 - x1) div 2 - TextW div 2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; TY := y1 + (y2 - y1) div 2 - TextH div 2 - 3;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Canvas.Font.Size := ScaleRound(Scale, Font_Size);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1045;&#1089;&#1083;&#1080; &#1096;&#1080;&#1088;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072; &#1080;&#1083;&#1080; &#1074;&#1099;&#1089;&#1086;&#1090;&#1072; &#1073;&#1083;&#1086;&#1082;&#1072; &#1084;&#1077;&#1085;&#1100;&#1096;&#1077;, &#1095;&#1077;&#1084; &#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1089;&#1090;&#1072;, &#1090;&#1086; &#1087;&#1086;&#1076;&#1075;&#1086;&#1085;&#1103;&#1077;&#1084; &#1087;&#1086;&#1076; &#1088;&#1072;&#1079;&#1084;&#1077;&#1088; &#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1089;&#1090;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(x2 - x1) &lt; TextW) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; x1 := x1 - textw div 2 - 10;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; x2 := x2 + textw div 2 + 10;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (abs(y2 - y1) &lt; TextH) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; y1 := y1 - textH div 2 - 10;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; y2 := y2 + textH div 2 + 10;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isVertex then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1056;&#1080;&#1089;&#1091;&#1077;&#1084; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1096;&#1080;&#1085;&#1099;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point.x := x1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point.y := y1;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point.y := y2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point.x := x2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point.y := y1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Canvas.Font.Size := ScaleRound(Scale, Font_Size);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Canvas.TextOut(ScaleRound(Scale, TX),ScaleRound(Scale, TY), text);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; temp := temp^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawSelectFigure(canvas:tcanvas; figure: TFigureInfo);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var x1,x2,y1,y2: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">point: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; x1 := figure.x1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; x2 := figure.x2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; y1 := figure.y1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; y2 := figure.y2;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Point.x := x1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Point.y := y1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point, clGreen);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Point.y := y2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point, clGreen);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Point.x := x2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point, clGreen);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Point.y := y1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas, Point, clGreen);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawSelectLineVertex(canvas: TCanvas; Point: TPointsInfo);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawVertexRect(canvas,Point, clGreen);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c63">end.</span></p><p class="c25 c12"><span class="c45"></span></p><p class="c25"><span class="c45">&#1052;&#1086;&#1076;&#1091;&#1083;&#1100; View.SVG</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">unit View.SVG;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">interface</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">uses Data.Types, Data.InitData;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure exportToSVG(head: PFigList; w,h: Integer; path:UTF8String; title: UTF8String; desc: UTF8String);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">implementation</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">uses SysUtils, vcl.dialogs, vcl.graphics, Model, View.Canvas, main, Model.Lines;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1047;&#1072;&#1075;&#1086;&#1083;&#1086;&#1074;&#1086;&#1082; SVG</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">const svg_head = &#39;&lt;?xml version=&quot;1.0&quot; standalone=&quot;no&quot;?&gt;&#39; + #10#13</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;+ &#39;&lt;!DOCTYPE svg PUBLIC &quot;-//W3C//DTD SVG 1.1//EN&quot;&#39;+ #10#13</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; + &#39;&quot;http://www.w3.org/Graphics/SVG/1.1/DTD/svg11.dtd&quot;&gt;&#39;;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1042;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1090; &#1089;&#1090;&#1088;&#1086;&#1082;&#1091; &#1089; &#1086;&#1090;&#1082;&#1088;&#1099;&#1090;&#1080;&#1077;&#1084; SVG-&#1090;&#1077;&#1075;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function getSVGOpenTag(h,w: integer):UTF8String;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; result := &#39;&lt;svg width=&quot;&#39; + IntToStr(W) + &#39;&quot; height=&quot;&#39; + IntToStr(H) + #10#13</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; + &#39;&quot; viewBox=&quot;0 0 &#39; + IntToStr(W) + &#39; &#39; + IntToStr(h) + &#39;&quot;&#39; + #10#13</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; + &#39;xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&quot; version=&quot;1.1&quot;&gt;&#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function writePatch(Point1, Point2: TPointsInfo; color: UTF8String = &#39;black&#39;; width:Integer = Default_LineSVG_Width):UTF8String;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Result := &#39;&lt;path d=&quot;M &#39; + IntToStr(Point1.x) + &#39; &#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; + IntToStr(Point1.y) + &nbsp; &#39; L &#39; + IntToStr(Point2.x)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; + &#39; &#39;+ IntToStr(Point2.y) + &#39;&quot; &#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; + &#39;fill=&quot;none&quot; stroke=&quot;&#39; + color +&#39;&quot; stroke-width=&quot;&#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; + IntToStr(width) + &#39;&quot; /&gt;&#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1060;&#1091;&#1085;&#1082;&#1094;&#1080;&#1103; &#1074;&#1086;&#1079;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1090; &#1089;&#1090;&#1088;&#1086;&#1082;&#1091; &#1089; text-&#1090;&#1077;&#1075;&#1086;&#1084; &#1089; &#1079;&#1072;&#1076;&#1072;&#1085;&#1085;&#1099;&#1084; &#1089;&#1086;&#1076;&#1077;&#1088;&#1078;&#1072;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077;&#1084;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function writeSVGText(Figure: TFigureInfo; text: UTF8String; family:UTF8String =</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &#39;Tahoma&#39;; size:integer = 16):UTF8String;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var TH, TW, TX,TY: real;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">TextW, TextH: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">const</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; SVG_VerticalEpsilon = 4; // &#1055;&#1086;&#1075;&#1088;&#1077;&#1096;&#1085;&#1086;&#1089;&#1090;&#1100; (&#1056;&#1072;&#1089;&#1089;&#1090;&#1086;&#1103;&#1085;&#1080;&#1077; &#1086;&#1090; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1093;&#1085;&#1077;&#1081; &#1090;&#1086;&#1095;&#1082;&#1080; &#1073;&#1091;&#1082;&#1074;&#1099; &#1076;&#1086;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;// &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1093;&#1072; &#1074;&#1099;&#1076;&#1077;&#1083;&#1103;&#1077;&#1084;&#1086;&#1081; &#1086;&#1073;&#1083;&#1072;&#1089;&#1090;&#1080; &#1073;&#1086;&#1083;&#1100;&#1096;&#1077;, &#1095;&#1077;&#1084; &#1076;&#1086; &#1085;&#1080;&#1078;&#1085;&#1077;&#1081;)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; with figure do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; // &#1050;&#1086;&#1086;&#1088;&#1076;&#1080;&#1085;&#1072;&#1090;&#1099; &#1094;&#1077;&#1085;&#1090;&#1088;&#1072; &#1087;&#1088;&#1103;&#1084;&#1086;&#1091;&#1075;&#1086;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1080;&#1082;&#1072;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; TX := x1 + abs(x2 - x1) / 2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; TY := y1 + abs(y2 - y1) / 2 + SVG_VerticalEpsilon;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; {&#39;&lt;rect x=&quot;&#39; + IntToStr(figure.x1) +&#39;&quot; y=&quot;&#39; + IntToStr(figure.y1) + &#39;&quot;&#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; + &#39; width=&quot;&#39;+ IntToStr(figure.x2-figure.x1) + &#39;&quot; height=&quot;&#39;+ IntToStr(figure.y2-figure.y1) + &#39;&quot;&#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; + &#39; style=&quot;fill:blue;stroke:pink;stroke-width:0;fill-opacity:0.1;stroke-opacity:0.9&quot; /&gt;&#39;}</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Result:=</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; // &nbsp;text-anchor=&quot;middle&quot; - &#1094;&#1077;&#1085;&#1090;&#1088;&#1080;&#1088;&#1091;&#1077;&#1090; &#1090;&#1077;&#1082;&#1089;&#1090; &#1087;&#1086; &#1074;&#1077;&#1088;&#1090;&#1080;&#1082;&#1072;&#1083;&#1080; &#1080; &#1075;&#1086;&#1088;&#1080;&#1079;&#1086;&#1085;&#1090;&#1072;&#1083;&#1080; &#1086;&#1090;&#1085;&#1086;&#1089;&#1080;&#1090;&#1077;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1086;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; // &nbsp;&#1086;&#1087;&#1088;&#1077;&#1076;&#1077;&#1083;&#1077;&#1085;&#1085;&#1086;&#1081; &#1090;&#1086;&#1095;&#1082;&#1080;. &#1055;&#1086;&#1076;&#1088;&#1086;&#1073;&#1085;&#1077;&#1077; - &#1074; &#1076;&#1086;&#1082;&#1091;&#1084;&#1077;&#1085;&#1090;&#1072;&#1094;&#1080;&#1080; &#1087;&#1086; &#1092;&#1086;&#1088;&#1084;&#1072;&#1090;&#1091; SVG</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &#39;&lt;text text-anchor=&quot;middle&quot; font-family = &quot;&#39;+ family +&#39;&quot; font-size = &quot;&#39; + IntToStr(size) + &#39;&quot;&#39;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; + &#39; x=&quot;&#39;+ StringReplace(FormatFloat( &#39;#.####&#39;, TX),&#39;,&#39;, &#39;.&#39;, [rfReplaceAll])</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; +&#39;&quot; y=&quot;&#39;+StringReplace(FormatFloat( &#39;#.####&#39;, TY),&#39;,&#39;, &#39;.&#39;, [rfReplaceAll])</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; +&#39;&quot;&gt;&#39; + text + &#39;&lt;/text&gt;&#39;;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawSVGBoundLine(var f: TextFile; FirstP: TPointsInfo; tmp:PPointsList; var lastp:PPointsList);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; coef: -1..1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P1, P2: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if FirstP.y - tmp^.adr^.Info.y &lt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; coef := 1</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; coef := -1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p1.x:= tmp^.Info.x-Lines_DegLenght;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p1.y := tmp^.Info.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.x := &nbsp;tmp^.Info.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.y := tmp^.Info.y+coef*Lines_Deg;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- BOUND LINE --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(p1, p2));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; lastp^.Info := p2;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawSVGArrowVertical(var f: textFile; x,y : integer; coef: ShortInt);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p1, p2: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; // Draw Vertical Arrow</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P1.x := x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P1.y := y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P2.x := x-Arrow_Height;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P2.y:= y+Arrow_Width*coef;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- ARROS LEFT --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(p1,p2));</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.x := x+Arrow_Height;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.y := y+Arrow_Width*coef;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- ARROW RIGHT --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(p1,p2));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawSVGArrow(var F: TextFile; x,y : integer; coef: ShortInt);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p1, p2: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P1.x := x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P1.y := y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P2.x := x-Arrow_Width*coef;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; P2.y:= y-Arrow_Height;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- ARROS LEFT --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(p1,p2));</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.x := &nbsp;x-Arrow_Width*coef;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.y := y+ +Arrow_Height;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- ARROW RIGHT --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(p1,p2));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1055;&#1088;&#1077;&#1074;&#1088;&#1072;&#1097;&#1072;&#1077;&#1084; &#1089;&#1087;&#1077;&#1094;&#1080;&#1072;&#1083;&#1100;&#1085;&#1099;&#1077; &#1089;&#1080;&#1084;&#1074;&#1086;&#1083;&#1099; &#1074; &quot;&#1089;&#1091;&#1097;&#1085;&#1086;&#1089;&#1090;&#1080;&quot;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">function htmlspecialchars(s: UTF8String):UTF8String;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp;s:=StringReplace(s,&#39;&amp;&#39;,&#39;&amp;amp;&#39;,[rfReplaceAll, rfIgnoreCase]);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp;s:=StringReplace(s,&#39;&lt;&#39;,&#39;&amp;lt;&#39;,[rfReplaceAll, rfIgnoreCase]);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp;s:=StringReplace(s,&#39;&gt;&#39;,&#39;&amp;gt;&#39;,[rfReplaceAll, rfIgnoreCase]);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp;s:=StringReplace(s,&#39;&quot;&#39;,&#39;&amp;quot;&#39;,[rfReplaceAll, rfIgnoreCase]);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp;result:=s;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawArrowAtSVG(var f: textfile; point, PrevPoint:TPointsInfo);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpx, tmpy:integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpx := point.x - PrevPoint.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if tmpx &gt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; drawSVGArrow(f,point.x, point.y,1)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else if tmpx &lt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; drawSVGArrow(f,point.x, point.y,-1);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpy := point.y - PrevPoint.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; if tmpy &gt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; drawSVGArrowVertical(f,point.x, point.y,-1)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; else if tmpy &lt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawSVGArrowVertical(f,point.x, point.y,1);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure drawIncomingLineSVG(var f: textfile; point: TPointsInfo; coef: ShortInt; var d: PPointsList);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p1,p2: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; point.y := point.y - coef*Lines_DegLenght;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p1 := point;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2:= point;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.y := p2.y + (Lines_Deg*coef);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p1 := p2;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.x := point.x+Lines_DegLenght;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; p2.y := point.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- Incoming Line --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(p1,p2));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; drawSVGArrowVertical(f, point.x, point.y+Lines_DegLenght*coef, coef);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; {point.y := point.y + 2*coef*Lines_DegLenght;}</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">// &#1069;&#1082;&#1089;&#1087;&#1086;&#1088;&#1090; &#1074; SVG</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">procedure exportToSVG(head: PFigList; w,h: Integer; path:UTF8String; title: UTF8String; desc: UTF8String);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">var</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; f: TextFile;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; Point1, Point2: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp: PFigList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpx: integer;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmpP, prevP: PPointsList;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; firstP: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; isFirstLine,isDegEnd :Boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; coef: ShortInt;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; text: UTF8String;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; prev: TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; curr:TPointsInfo;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; isChanged: boolean;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; AssignFile(f, path,CP_UTF8);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; rewrite(f);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, svg_head);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, getSVGOpenTag(h,w));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;title&gt;&#39; + title + &#39;&lt;/title&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; tmp := head^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; while tmp &lt;&gt; nil do</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if tmp^.Info.tp = line then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP := tmp^.Info.PointHead^.adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prevp := tmpP;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; curr := tmpP^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; firstP := tmpP^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isFirstLine := false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if beginOfVertLine(tmpP,firstP) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prev := prevP^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawSVGBoundLine(f, firstp, tmpP, prevp);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- Line After Bound --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Writeln(f, writePatch(prevP^.Info, tmpP^.adr.Info));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prevP^.Info := prev;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP := tmpP^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isFirstLine := &nbsp;true;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isChanged := false;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if isHorisontalIntersection(EditorForm.getFigureHead,tmpP) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (tmpP^.Adr &lt;&gt; nil) and (FirstP.x - tmpP^.adr^.Info.x &lt; 0) then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coef := 1</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; coef := -1;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point2 := tmpP^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point2.x := tmpP^.Info.x+Lines_Deg*coef;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- Additional line Intersection: --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(Point1,Point2,&#39;black&#39;));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; isChanged := true;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; if not isChanged then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prev := tmpP^.Info</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prev := curr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; prevp := tmpP;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; tmpP := tmpP^.Adr;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; curr := tmpP^.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (tmpP^.Adr = nil) and &nbsp;isHorisontalIntersection(EditorForm.getFigureHead,tmpP) &nbsp;then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; begin</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point1 := prevP.Info;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Point2.x := curr.x-Lines_Deg*coef;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point2.y := curr.y;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writeln(f, &#39;&lt;!-- Additional line: --&gt;&#39;);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; writeln(f, writePatch(Point1,Point2,&#39;black&#39;));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if Prev.x - curr.x &gt; 0 then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawSVGArrow(f, curr.x-Lines_Deg*coef, curr.y, -1)</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; else</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; drawSVGArrow(f, curr.x-Lines_Deg*coef, curr.y, 1);</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point1.x := curr.x;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; point1.y := curr.y+Lines_DegLenght;</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; Writeln(f, writePatch( prev, curr));</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; if (tmpP^.Adr = nil) and isDegEnd and (prevP^.Info.x = curr.x) &nbsp;then</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; end;</span></p><p class="c4 c12"><span class="c6"></span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;if needMiddleArrow(tmpp, FirstP) then // if these is incoming and outgoing lines</span></p><p class="c4"><span class="c6">&nbsp;
